CREATE TABLE players
(playerId INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT, NAME VARCHAR(255),Nation VARCHAR(255),Pos VARCHAR(255),Squad VARCHAR(255), SquadId INT, Age INT, Born INT, MP INT, Starts INT, Min INT, 90s INT, Gls INT, Ast INT, G-PK INT, PK INT, PKatt INT, CrdY VARCHAR(255),CrdR VARCHAR(255),GlsP90 VARCHAR(255), AstP90 VARCHAR(255),G+AP90 VARCHAR(255),G-PKP90 VARCHAR(255),G+A-PKP90 VARCHAR(255),xG VARCHAR(255),npxG VARCHAR(255),xA VARCHAR(255),npxG+xA VARCHAR(255),xGP90 VARCHAR(255),xAP90 VARCHAR(255), xG+xAP90 VARCHAR(255), npxGP90 VARCHAR(255), npxG+xAP90 VARCHAR(255), PRIMARY KEY (playerId))

CREATE TABLE players
(playerId INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY, Name VARCHAR(255),Nation VARCHAR(255),Pos VARCHAR(255),Squad VARCHAR(255), SquadId INT, Age INT, Born INT, MP INT, Starts INT, Min INT, 90s INT, Gls INT, Ast INT, GPK INT, PK INT, PKatt INT, CrdY VARCHAR(255),CrdR VARCHAR(255),GlsP90 VARCHAR(255), AstP90 VARCHAR(255), GAP90 VARCHAR(255), GPKP90 VARCHAR(255),GAPKP90 VARCHAR(255),xG VARCHAR(255),npxG VARCHAR(255),xA VARCHAR(255),npxGxA VARCHAR(255), xGP90 VARCHAR(255), xAP90 VARCHAR(255), xGxAP90 VARCHAR(255), npxGP90 VARCHAR(255), npxGxAP90 VARCHAR(255))

//WHAT IM USING
CREATE TABLE players
(playerId INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY, Name VARCHAR(255),Nation VARCHAR(255),Position VARCHAR(255),Team VARCHAR(255), TeamId INT, Age INT, Born INT, Matches INT, Starts INT, Minutes INT, 90mins INT, Goals INT, Assists INT, NonPenGoals INT, PenGoals INT, PenAttempts INT, Yellows INT, Reds INT, GlsPer90 VARCHAR(255), AstPer90 VARCHAR(255), GlsAstPer90 VARCHAR(255), NonPenGoalsPer90 VARCHAR(255),NonPenGlsAstPer90 VARCHAR(255),xG VARCHAR(255),NonPenxG VARCHAR(255),xA VARCHAR(255),npxGxA VARCHAR(255), xGPer90 VARCHAR(255), xAPer90 VARCHAR(255), xGxAPer90 VARCHAR(255), npxGPer90 VARCHAR(255), npxGxAPer90 VARCHAR(255))

(Name, Nation, Position, Team, TeamId, Age, Born, Matches, Starts, Minutes, 90mins, Goals, Assists, NonPenGoals, PenGoals , PenAttempts, Yellows ,Reds ,GlsPer90 , AstPer90, GlsAstPer90, NonPenGoalsPer90, NonPenGlsAstPer90, xG, NonPenxG, xA ,npxGxA , xGPer90 , xAPer90 , xGxAPer90 , npxGPer90, npxGxAPer90)


CREATE TABLE teams
(teamId INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,    
teamName VARCHAR(255), 
imageUrl VARCHAR(255), 
league VARCHAR(255), 
leagueId INT, 
manager VARCHAR(255),
location VARCHAR(255),
stadium VARCHAR(255),
capacity INT)
